# Freight Hub Stopping Range

## Dataset

| Name | Value |
| :--- | :---- |
| Catalog | [Link](https://catalog.data.gov/dataset/freight-hub-stopping-range) |

| Data: JSON | [100 Rows](https://data.iowa.gov/api/views/qa57-wpne/rows.json?max_rows=100) |
| Data: CSV | [100 Rows](https://data.iowa.gov/api/views/qa57-wpne/rows.csv?max_rows=100) |
| Host | data.iowa.gov |
| Id | qa57-wpne |
| Name | Freight Hub Stopping Range |
| Attribution | Iowa DOT, HDR Engineering |
| Category | Transportation & Utilities |

| Created | 2016-08-19T21:21:37Z |
| Publication Date | 2016-08-19T21:23:08Z |

## Description

Iowa Department of Transportation statewide rest area data. This layer displays freight hub stopping ranges.

## Columns

```ls
| Included | Schema Type    | Field Name            | Name                  | Data Type  | Render Type |
| ======== | ============== | ===================== | ===================== | ========== | =========== |
| No       | time           | :updated_at           | updated_at            | meta_data  | meta_data   |
| Yes      | series tag     | objectid              | OBJECTID              | text       | number      |
| No       |                | shape                 | SHAPE                 | geospatial | geospatial  |
| Yes      | series tag     | route_name            | Route_Name            | text       | text        |
| Yes      | series tag     | corridor              | Corridor              | text       | text        |
| Yes      | series tag     | ten_hour_direction    | Ten_Hour_Direction    | text       | text        |
| Yes      | numeric metric | mile_marker           | Mile_Marker           | number     | text        |
| Yes      | series tag     | corridor_2            | Corridor_2            | text       | text        |
| Yes      | series tag     | eleven_hour_direction | Eleven_Hour_Direction | text       | text        |
| Yes      | numeric metric | mile_marker_2         | Mile_Marker_2         | number     | text        |
```
